  534 | function buildGeminiHistoryContents(
  535 |   messages: GeminiHistoryMessage[],

  537 |   const normalized: Array<{
  538 |     role: 'user' | 'model'
  539 |     text: string
  540 |   }> = []
  541 | 
  542 |   for (const message of messages) {
  543 |     const cleanText =
  544 |       message.content.trim()
  545 | 
  546 |     if (!cleanText) {
  547 |       continue
  548 |     }
  549 | 
  550 |     const role =
  551 |       message.role === 'assistant'
  552 |         ? 'model'
  553 |         : 'user'
  554 |

  556 |       normalized.at(-1)

  534 | function buildGeminiHistoryContents(
  535 |   messages: GeminiHistoryMessage[],
  536 | ): Content[] {
  537 |   const normalized: Array<{
  538 |     role: 'user' | 'model'
  539 |     text: string
  540 |   }> = []
  541 | 
  542 |   for (const message of messages) {
  543 |     const cleanText =
  544 |       message.content.trim()
  545 | 
  546 |     if (!cleanText) {
  547 |       continue
  548 |     }
  549 | 
  550 |     const role =
  551 |       message.role === 'assistant'
  552 |         ? 'model'
  553 |         : 'user'
  554 | 
  555 |     const previous =
  556 |       normalized.at(-1)
  557 | 
  558 |     if (previous?.role === role) {
  559 |       previous.text =
  560 |         previous.text +
  561 |         '\n\n' +
  562 |         cleanText
  563 | 
  564 |       continue
  565 |     }
  566 | 
  567 |     normalized.push({

  569 |       text: cleanText,
  570 |     })
